! Splitting into name types
! =========================

! When the dust has settled, these 5 types will be joined into one 
! alphabetical list. They are separated in this initial phase in order
! to make uniform treatment of each type easier.

LEXICON Propernouns

 mal ; ! Male first names
 fem ; ! Female first names
 plc ; ! Place names and other names
 sur ; ! Surnames
! org ; ! Organisations
! manuallyaddednames ; ! Manually added Faroese place names.

! Manually added names.

!LEXICON manuallyaddednames
